  <script type="text/javascript">
   jQuery(document).ready(function() {
				// CUSTOM AJAX CONTENT LOADING FUNCTION
				var ajaxRevslider = function(obj) {
				
					// obj.type : Post Type
					// obj.id : ID of Content to Load
					// obj.aspectratio : The Aspect Ratio of the Container / Media
					// obj.selector : The Container Selector where the Content of Ajax will be injected. It is done via the Essential Grid on Return of Content
					
					var content = "";

					data = {};
					
					data.action = 'revslider_ajax_call_front';
					data.client_action = 'get_slider_html';
					data.token = '505d00bc2e';
					data.type = obj.type;
					data.id = obj.id;
					data.aspectratio = obj.aspectratio;
					
					// SYNC AJAX REQUEST
					jQuery.ajax({
						type:"post",
						url:"http://blog.graphicstock.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php",
						dataType: 'json',
						data:data,
						async:false,
						success: function(ret, textStatus, XMLHttpRequest) {
							if(ret.success == true)
								content = ret.data;								
						},
						error: function(e) {
							console.log(e);
						}
					});
					
					 // FIRST RETURN THE CONTENT WHEN IT IS LOADED !!
					 return content;						 
				};
				
				// CUSTOM AJAX FUNCTION TO REMOVE THE SLIDER
				var ajaxRemoveRevslider = function(obj) {
					return jQuery(obj.selector+" .rev_slider").revkill();
				};

				// EXTEND THE AJAX CONTENT LOADING TYPES WITH TYPE AND FUNCTION
				var extendessential = setInterval(function() {
					if (jQuery.fn.tpessential != undefined) {
						clearInterval(extendessential);
						if(typeof(jQuery.fn.tpessential.defaults) !== 'undefined') {
							jQuery.fn.tpessential.defaults.ajaxTypes.push({type:"revslider",func:ajaxRevslider,killfunc:ajaxRemoveRevslider,openAnimationSpeed:0.3});   
							// type:  Name of the Post to load via Ajax into the Essential Grid Ajax Container
							// func: the Function Name which is Called once the Item with the Post Type has been clicked
							// killfunc: function to kill in case the Ajax Window going to be removed (before Remove function !
							// openAnimationSpeed: how quick the Ajax Content window should be animated (default is 0.3)
						}
					}
				},30);
			});
  </script>

          </a>

          <i class="fa fa-file-text">
          </i>
         </span>
        </header>
        <div class="post-body">
         <p class="no-break">
          <span class="st_facebook_large" st_title="Smart Infographics: Easy Design Hacks" st_url="http://blog.graphicstock.com/graphic-design-trends/smart-infographics-easy-design-hacks/">
          </span>
          <span class="st_twitter_large" st_title="Smart Infographics: Easy Design Hacks" st_url="http://blog.graphicstock.com/graphic-design-trends/smart-infographics-easy-design-hacks/" st_username="graphicstock_" st_via="graphicstock_">
          </span>
          <span class="st_linkedin_large" st_title="Smart Infographics: Easy Design Hacks" st_url="http://blog.graphicstock.com/graphic-design-trends/smart-infographics-easy-design-hacks/">
          </span>
          <span class="st_pinterest_large" st_title="Smart Infographics: Easy Design Hacks" st_url="http://blog.graphicstock.com/graphic-design-trends/smart-infographics-easy-design-hacks/">
          </span>
          <span class="st_plusone_large" st_title="Smart Infographics: Easy Design Hacks" st_url="http://blog.graphicstock.com/graphic-design-trends/smart-infographics-easy-design-hacks/">
          </span>
          <span class="st_email_large" st_title="Smart Infographics: Easy Design Hacks" st_url="http://blog.graphicstock.com/graphic-design-trends/smart-infographics-easy-design-hacks/">
          </span>
         </p>
         <h2>
          Smart Infographics: Easy Design Hacks
         </h2>
         <p>
          <b>
           Using Every Pixel to Your Advantage
          </b>
         </p>
         <p>
          Theres a very mindful reason behind our offering
          <a href="http://www.graphicstock.com/search/infographic/everything/?utm_medium=content&amp;utm_campaign=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214&amp;utm_source=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214" target="_blank" title="infographic templates">
           infographic templates
          </a>
          in editable vector format and pairing them with minimal backgrounds: so that you the designer can easily adapt them to fit your own thematic needs.
         </p>
         <p>
          If youre in urgent need of an abstract or psychology-themed infographic design, weve got you covered with plenty of existing pre-fab templates:
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://www.graphicstock.com/stock-image/simply-minimal-infographic-template-design-vector-52806.html?utm_medium=content&amp;utm_campaign=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214&amp;utm_source=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214" target="_blank">
           <img alt="239-1013-A0242" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-392" height="300" src="http://d2436y6oj07al2.cloudfront.net/assets/gsblog/2014/01/239-1013-A0242-300x300.jpg" width="300"/>
          </a>
          <a href="http://www.graphicstock.com/stock-image/3d-modern-white-design-template-for-infographics.html?utm_medium=content&amp;utm_campaign=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214&amp;utm_source=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214" target="_blank">
           <img alt="3d-modern-white-design-template-for-infographics-913-34" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-393" height="300" src="http://d2436y6oj07al2.cloudfront.net/assets/gsblog/2014/01/3d-modern-white-design-template-for-infographics-913-34-300x300.jpg" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          But what if youre tasked with designing an infographic for an article on
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2010/11/11/apps-for-ski-and-snowboard/" target="_blank">
           available snowboarding apps
          </a>
          or as an advertisement for a ski resort?
         </p>
         <p>
          The entire concept behind creating infographics is to deliver complex information as easily and rapidly as possible. To accomplish this, you need to ensure youre using every pixel to your advantage. What does this mean in terms of design? It means audiences shouldnt have to study your infographic to identify the purpose behind it.
         </p>
         <p>
          <b>
           Saturating Your Theme
          </b>
         </p>
         <p>
          More specifically, this means that if your ultimate goal is to draw upon a readers love of skiing and snowboarding, you want to ensure youre triggering this impulse from a distance and not burying it behind small text and universal icons.
         </p>
         <p>
          The easiest way to do this? By taking a few minutes to turn a stock template into a custom template by adding additional textures and icons.
         </p>
         <p>
          <b>
           From Stock to Ski Slopes
          </b>
         </p>
         <p>
          To the left is one of our
          <a href="http://www.graphicstock.com/stock-image/blue-infographic-chart-template-vector.html?utm_medium=content&amp;utm_campaign=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214&amp;utm_source=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214" target="_blank">
           most popular infographic designs
          </a>
          prior to any modification. To the right, weve leveraged the same design alongside one of our
          <a href="http://www.graphicstock.com/stock-image/blue-snowy-mountains.html?utm_medium=content&amp;utm_campaign=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214&amp;utm_source=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214" target="_blank" title="mountain vectors">
           mountain vectors
          </a>
          and accented it with a few of our
          <a href="http://www.graphicstock.com/stock-image/skiing-silhouette.html?utm_medium=content&amp;utm_campaign=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214&amp;utm_source=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214" target="_blank" title="ski silhouettes">
           skier
          </a>
          and
          <a href="http://www.graphicstock.com/stock-image/snowboarding-silhouette.html?utm_medium=content&amp;utm_campaign=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214&amp;utm_source=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214" target="_blank" title="snowboarding silhouette">
           snowboarder silhouettes
          </a>
          :
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://www.graphicstock.com/stock-image/blue-infographic-chart-template-vector.html?utm_medium=content&amp;utm_campaign=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214&amp;utm_source=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214" target="_blank">
           <img alt="infographic1" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-394" height="300" src="http://d2436y6oj07al2.cloudfront.net/assets/gsblog/2014/01/infographic1-300x300.jpg" width="300"/>
          </a>
          <a href="http://www.graphicstock.com/stock-image/blue-snowy-mountains.html?utm_medium=content&amp;utm_campaign=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214&amp;utm_source=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214" target="_blank">
           <img alt="info2" class="alignnone wp-image-395" height="300" src="http://d2436y6oj07al2.cloudfront.net/assets/gsblog/2014/01/info2-207x300.jpg" width="207"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          Which do you think will prove more effective in terms of grabbing a snowboard enthusiasts attention from afar?
         </p>
         <p>
          And how can you modify your next infographic to gain the same advantage?
         </p>
         <p>
          Existing members can download all of the content sourced above by searching
          <a href="http://www.graphicstock.com/search/infographic/everything/?utm_medium=content&amp;utm_campaign=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214&amp;utm_source=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214" target="_blank">
           infographic
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://www.graphicstock.com/search/mountain/everything/?utm_medium=content&amp;utm_campaign=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214&amp;utm_source=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214" target="_blank">
           mountain
          </a>
          , and
          <a href="http://www.graphicstock.com/image/tags/silhouette/?utm_medium=content&amp;utm_campaign=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214&amp;utm_source=GSBlogSmartInfographics0214" target="_blank">
           silhouette
          </a>
          in our library.
         </p>
         <p style="padding-top: 1em;">
          <i>
           Want to request additional infographic tips and tutorials? Email your questions and requests to social@videoblocks.com
          </i>
         </p>
         [cta]
        </div>
        <div class="row">
